Post Production / Delivery Intern

A24 · New York, NY (On-site)

About the job

A24 is seeking to hire a Post Production / Delivery intern to support the team. Must be available 2 days in the NY office, up to 15 hours per week.This is an in-person internship in our Manhattan office.Initial ResponsibilitiesPost & Technical Delivery

  • Coordinate shipping and tracking deliveries
  • Take meeting notes as requested
  • Research Post and Delivery tools for future initiatives
  • Compress EPK footage, handle transcriptions of EPK’s and trailers, distribute links as needed
  • Pull clean clips for marketing use, trailers, TV spots and social assets
  • Pull high res stills from ProRes files for print vendors
  • Download, ingest and watermark various video files and documents
  • Assist with reviewing localization assets for accuracy
  • Assist with anti-piracy initiatives
  • Assist with home entertainment metadata, as needed
  • Assist with QC picture/audio assets, as needed
Archive Management
  • Update inventories as assets get moved between facilities
  • Reach out to labs for archival materials
  • Log and organize film documents and drives
Qualifications
  • Able to work in-office in our New York office
  • 1+ years in post-production environment, or relevant internship experience
  • Strong attention to detail and follow through skills
  • Proficient in Adobe Premiere Pro, Microsoft Office, Shipping and Receiving
We are looking for diverse perspectives. A24 is an Equal Opportunity Employer and encourages applications from all kinds of candidates.Our internships are part-time roles with an hourly rate of $18.00.A24 is an acclaimed global entertainment company known for producing and distributing films, television series, documentaries, music, publishing, and consumer products. Established in New York in 2012, A24 has cultivated a library of over 150 films and 50 TV series, earning critical and commercial acclaim with more than 21 Oscars, 18 Golden Globes, and 18 Emmys. Renowned for groundbreaking hits likeMoonlight, Everything Everywhere All at Once,andUncut Gems, as well as television successes such asEuphoria, Beef,andRamy, A24 has developed a passionate fanbase and expanded into ventures like Half Magic and the Cherry Lane theater. Upcoming projects includeMarty Supremestarring Timothée Chalamet and Gwyneth Paltrow,The Dramastarring Zendaya and Robert Pattinson,The Smashing Machinestarring Dwayne “The Rock” Johnson and Emily Blunt,Materialistsstarring Chris Evans, Pedro Pascal and Dakota Johnson, andEddingtonstarring Joaquin Phoenix, Pedro Pascal, and Emma Stone, among others.All valid links to open A24 job opportunities can be found at https://a24films.com/jobs or the Company's official Linkedin page. Official recruiting communications will come only through emails from the domain @a24films.com.
